54b2(dkon brtsegs): ngo mtshar dang slad du shes bskyed de/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i skabasam gyi mi khyab pa la mngon par dad/

54b5(dkon brtsegs): de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / 'al 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od bsam gyis mi khyab

55a1(dkon brtsegs): gas ma pan

55b1(dkon brtsegs): ba sams kyi mi khyab pa// thams cad du ni chos sgrog ste/ sangs rgyas kyi ni spyod yul dang // ci tsam sems can thams cad kyi// dus gsum dag gi dbang //
55b2(dkon brtsegs): kun// sangs rgyas kyis ni rab mkhyen te// bsam mi khyab lab tu dang // sangs rgyas rnams kyi 'od mtha' yas// 'od zer dra ba bsam mi khyab// zhing

100a5(dkon brtsegs): su mthun sgra dang / nang du tshul bzhin lta ba'o// tshul bzhin rgyu ni zhi gnas te/ lhag mthong yang ni rkyen yin no// sems can gang gis 'gro 'gyur la/ de yang
100a6(dkon brtsegs): 'dren pas rab tu mkhyen/ tshul khrims la ni rnal 'byor gnas/ chos rnams rtong pa rab tu rtogs/ mthar pa'i lam ni sgom pas na/ srid pa dog las thar
100a7(dkon brtsegs): bar 'gyur/ de dag sangs rgyas rab mkhyen nas/ rnam sbyor skyes pa bu med la/ spong pa nyid dang mtshan med dang / rnam par thar pa rab tu ston/ ngas ma
100a8(dkon brtsegs): gtan la ni snyoms zhugs pa/ rang rgyal dang ni nyan thos rnams/ de dag rnams kyang dog par bshad/ de ni 'gran zla yod par gsungs/ sangs rgyas bsam
100b1(dkon brtsegs): gtan rnam thar la/ dgra dang bcas med dog pa med/ sangs rgyas kyi ni stobs bdun dang / pha rol rgol bas thub pa dka'/ sha ri'i bu 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa
100b2(dkon brtsegs): rnams kyi/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bdun pa ste/ stobs de dang ldan pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa khyu mchod gi gnas su zhal gyi 'che ba nas/ sus kyang 'jig rten
100b3(dkon brtsegs): 'dir chos dang mthun pa zhes bya ba'i bar du'o// de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyis gnas rjes su dran pas mngon sum du byed pa/ mkhyen pa'i stobs gang zhe na/ 'di
100b4(dkon brtsegs): la sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pas bla na med pa yang dag pa'i ye shes kyis bdag dang sems can gzhan rnams dang / gang zag gzhan dag gis sngon gyis gnas rnam pa du ma
100b5(dkon brtsegs): rje su dran no// 'di lta ste/ skye ba gcig gam/ gnyis sam/ gsum 'am/ bzhi'am/ lnga 'am bcu 'am/ nyi shu 'am/ sum bcu 'am/ bzhi bcu 'am/ skye ba stong ngam/
100b6(dkon brtsegs): skye ba bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gi bar du rjes su dran no// 'jig pa'i bskal pa 'am/ chags pa'i bskal pa dam 'am/ 'jig pa dang chags pa'i bskal pa du ma zhig na
100b7(dkon brtsegs): nga sngon che ge mo zhig byung ste/ ming ni 'di zhe bya/ rus ni 'di zhes bya/ rigs ni 'di zhes bya/ kha zas ni 'di lta bu zhig za/ kha dog ni 'di lta du/ mtshan ma
100b8(dkon brtsegs): ni 'di lta bu/ dbyings ni 'di lta bu/ che ni 'di cham zhig thub/ yun ni 'di srid cig gnas nas/ bde ba dang sdug bsngal ni 'di lta du zhig myong te/ bdag de nas che
101a1(dkon brtsegs): du bya/ 'phos nas che ge bo zhig du skyes so// bdag de nas tshe 'phos nas 'dir skyes so zhes 'di lta bu rnams dang bcas/ yul phyogs
101a2(dkon brtsegs): dang bcas/ bzhi ci las gyur pa dang bcad par/ bdag dang gzhan gyi sngon gyi gnas da pa rjes su dran no// sems can gang gis sngon gyi rgyu ci lta bu dang / rgyu gang gi
101a3(dkon brtsegs): sems can du gyur pa'i rgyu de dang / de bzhin gsheg pas rab tu mkhyen to// mkhyen nas kyang de bzhin du chos ston to// 'das pa'i sems can thams cad kyis/
101a4(dkon brtsegs): 'das pa'i sems kyis rgyud kyang rab tu mkhyen to// / sems gang gi 'og tu gang la dmigs pa'i sems skyes pa dang / dmigs pa gang ma tshangs pas/
101a5(dkon brtsegs): 'gags pa de thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu mkhyen to// de ltar sha ri'i bu sems can gcig gi sems can cig nas cig tu sems 'di lta bu zhi
101a6(dkon brtsegs): 'og tu/ sems 'di lta bu zhig 'byung ngo zhes bya ba de ni/ bskal pa gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed du rlig gis bshad pas ston mi nus te de bzhin du sems can thams cad
101a7(dkon brtsegs): kyi yang thams cad de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu mkhyen to// mtha' mi'i mtha'i bar gyis bskal par de bzhin gshegs pas sems can de dag gi sems rnam
101a8(dkon brtsegs): par bshad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes mthar thug par mi 'gyur ro// de ltar sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa sngon sum du byed pa
101b1(dkon brtsegs): khyen pa'i stobs ni bas kyi mi khyab/ mtshungs pa med grangs med/ brjod du med/ de'i mtha' gnas ni bde bar bstan mi nus so// sangs rgyas kyi
101b2(dkon brtsegs): khyu mchog tu gyur pas de bzhin gshegs pa sems can de dag la/ sems can rnams dge ba'i rtsa ba de dang de/ sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'am/ nyan thos la bskyed
101b3(dkon brtsegs): pa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas la bskyed pa 'am/ chos la bskyed pa de dag dran par gyis shig/ ces dran par mdzad do// 'di lta ste/ de dag kyang sangs rgyas
101b4(dkon brtsegs): mthus dran par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pas de dag la dge ba'i rtsa ba la dmigs te chos 'di lta bur ston to// ci nas sems can de dag bla na med pa yang dag
101b5(dkon brtsegs): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi zlog par 'gyur zhing / mos ji lta ba bzhin du la la ni nyan thos kyi thegs pas/ la la ni rang sangs rgyas theg pas 'byung bar 'gyur
101b6(dkon brtsegs): la la ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do// de ltar rnyi'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa mngon sum byed pa shes pa'i
101b7(dkon brtsegs): stobs ni mtha' yas mu med/ namakha' dang mtshungs shing mnyam mo// byang chub sems dpas de thos nas mngon par dang / yid ches rab tu rtog soms nyid med/
101b8(dkon brtsegs): the tsom mi za ba nas/ na mkha' lta bu bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i bar du'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad gsungs te/ bde bar gshegs pas de skad/
102a1(dkon brtsegs): bka' stsal nas ston pas yang 'di skad gsung so// bdag gi dang ni de bzhin gshegs dag gis
102a2(dkon brtsegs): 'jig rten sgron mas sngon gyi dran pa ni/ bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig mtha' yas pa/ skyu rur lnga lag zil bzhag pa bzhin/ ming rus de bzhin kha dog rnam par rtog
102a3(dkon brtsegs): tshe dang gnas dang 'chi 'pho 'gro ba dang / gang gi rgyu sems can rgyud ldan pa/ dus mkhyen pa ni de la chos kyang 'chad/ 'gro ba rnams ni sems dang sems byang chos/
102a4(dkon brtsegs): chom gang dag 'das pa mtha' yas mu med pa/ gang gi 'og tu sems gang byung ba kun/ rgyal ba ye shes chen pos mnga' bas mkhyen/ sems can gcig gis
102a5(dkon brtsegs): sems rgyu sngon 'das pa/ bde bar gshegs pas rab tu mkhyen pa ni/ bskal pa gang gi klung gi bye ba snyed du/ bshad dang de'i mtha' mar phyin mi 'gyur/ sngon
102a6(dkon brtsegs): gyi spyod pa ci ste de dag ni/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bar du ngas bshad kyang / mtshungs pa med pa'i ye shes mi zad de/ bcom ldan ye shes rgya mtsho 'di 'dra'o// sngon gyi rgyal
102a7(dkon brtsegs): la sti stang gang byas shing / sems can gang dag dge ba'i bsam 'gyur ba/ sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul stobs kyi shugs la gnas/ sngon dag dge ba byas pa rnams kyang
102a8(dkon brtsegs): dran/ sngon gyi bsod nams ci 'dra byas pa rnams/ de dag rnams kyang ston pa'i bus dran te/ de dag dran nas ni gsum la 'khod/ mthar ba'i gnas la phyir yang mi sngo/
102b1(dkon brtsegs): 'gyur/ bde gshegs sngon gyi spong ba mtha' yas te/ sems can thams cad kyi ni bsam mi nas/ mtha' yas grags pa'i stobs ni brgyad pa la/ rgyal sras
102b2(dkon brtsegs): bdag nyid chen po dad par 'gyur/ sha ri'i bu 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs brgyad pa ste/ stobs de dang ldan pa zhes bya ba dang / chos
102b3(dkon brtsegs): mthun pa zhes bya ba dang / chos dang mthun pa zhes bya ba'i bar dri'o// de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i lha'i mig rjes su dran pa mngon sum du byed pa mkhyen pa'i stobs gang zhe na/
102b4(dkon brtsegs): 'di la sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pas bla na med pa'i ye shes dang / mi las shin tu 'das pa'i lha'i mig rnams par dag pas sems can rnams 'phro ba dang / skye ba dang /
102b5(dkon brtsegs): bzang po dang / ngan pa dang / kha dog mdzes pa dang / kha dog mi sdug pa dang / 'di 'gror 'gro ba dang / ngan 'gror 'gro ba rnams gzigs so// sems can 'di dag
102b6(dkon brtsegs): gis lus kyis nyes par spyod pa dang ldan/ ngag gi nyes par spyod pa dang / yid kyi nyes par spyod pa dang ldan pa/ 'phags pa la bskur pa 'debs pa/ log par lta ba
102b7(dkon brtsegs): dag ste/ de dag log par lta ba'i las yang dag pa'i blangs pa'i lus zhig te/ shi ba'i 'og tu ngan song ngan 'gror log par ltung ba sems can dmyal bar skye'o// dud
102b8(dkon brtsegs): 'gro skya gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten du yang de bzhin no// yang sems can 'di dag ni lus kyi legs par spyod pa dang ldan/ ngag gi legs par spyod pa dang
103a1(dkon brtsegs): ldan/ yid kyis legs par spyod pa dang ldan te/ 'phags pa rnams la bskur pa mi 'debs pa yang
103a2(dkon brtsegs): dag par lta ba ste/ de dag yang dag par blangs pa'i rgyus lus zhig nas/ bde 'gro mtho ris kyi 'jig rten du ltar skye'o// zhes sems can rnams kyi las ci ltar
103a3(dkon brtsegs): bsags pa rnams rab tu mkhyen to// de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i lha'i mig de ni phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing na mkha'i mtha' chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa/
103a4(dkon brtsegs): brjod du med pa gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed las kyang shin tu 'das pa thams cad na/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gang ci snyed snang bar 'gyur ba de dag thams cad ni tshig pa dang /
103a5(dkon brtsegs): 'jig pa dang / chags par gzigs so// sems can gang dag kha cig snang bar gyur pa de dag thams cad 'chi 'pho ba dang / skye bar gzigs so//
103a6(dkon brtsegs): byang chub sems dpas gang dag kha cig 'di la snang bar gyur pa de dag thams cad ni/ dga' ldan gnas nas 'chi 'pho dang / ma'i rum du 'jug pa dang / btsa'
103a7(dkon brtsegs): ba dang gom pa bdun 'dor ba dang / btsun po'i 'khor gyi nang 'jug pa dang / mngon par byung bar gzigs so// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang dag
103a8(dkon brtsegs): kha gcig snang bar 'gyur ba de dag thams cad ni byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas par gzigs so// chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba dang / yongs su ma
103b1(dkon brtsegs): ngan las 'da' bar yang gzigs so// nyan thos gang dag kha gcig snang bar gyur pa de dag thams cad ni shin du yongasu mya ngan las 'da' bar gzigs so// rang
103b2(dkon brtsegs): sangs rgyas gang dag kha cig snang bar gyur pa de thams cad ni/ rdzu 'phrul ston cing yon sbyong bar gzigs so// sems can gang dag snang bar ma gyur pa phyi rol gyi
103b3(dkon brtsegs): drang srong mngon par shes pa dang ldan pa rnams kyi mig gis lam du mi 'gro ba dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis kyang 'thob
103b4(dkon brtsegs): par mi 'gyur ba de dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i lha'i mig gis gzigs so// de yang de bzhin gshegs pas shing rta'i 'phang lo'i tshad tsam la snang bar ma gyur
103b5(dkon brtsegs): ba'i sems can rnams gzigs pa de dag ni shin tu mang gi/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi lha dang / mi rnams ni de lta ma yin te/ de ltar
103b6(dkon brtsegs): mi snang bar gyur pa'i sems can gyi khams kyang tshad med do// 'di ltar sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa ni lha'i mig gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing na sems can gang sangs
103b7(dkon brtsegs): rgyas kyi 'dul bar 'gyur zhes sems can gyi khams la gzigs ste/ sems can ci tsam sangs rgyas kyis 'dul bar 'gyur ba de dge mdun na de bzhin gshegs pas
103b8(dkon brtsegs): zhugs shing / sems can de dag 'dul yang sems can gzhan gyi mi shes so// de ltar na sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa'i lha'i mig rjes su dran pa mngon sum du byed
104a1(dkon brtsegs): pa mkhyen pa'i stobs ni mtha' ya sa mu med de namakha' dang mtshungs shing mnyam mo// byang chub sems
104a2(dkon brtsegs): dpa' pa de thos nas mngon par dad pa dang / nam mkha' lta bur bsam gyi mi khyab pa'i phyir zhes bya ba'i bar du'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don 'di nyid rgya cher
104a3(dkon brtsegs): bstan pa'i phyir/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gsungs so// bde bar gshegs pa'i lha'i mig dri med de/ bskal pa bye bar dge ba'i las kyi spangs/ des
104a4(dkon brtsegs): ni rgyal ba phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas zhing / rgya chen bsam gyis mi khyab rnams kyang gzigs/ 'byung ba dang ni 'jig pa ci snyed pa/ kha ci mi yis 'khor cing
104a5(dkon brtsegs): sems can gnas/ kha cig sangs rgyas ldan zhing kha cig stong / thams cad rang byung gi ni sman gyi gzigs/ sems cad khams ni rgya cher bsam mi khyab/
104a6(dkon brtsegs): gzugs can gzugs med gang dag ci snyed dang / gang dag ngan 'gror ltung dang bde 'gro ba/ thams cad rang byung gi ni spun gyis gzigs/ sangs rgyas bye ba mang
104a7(dkon brtsegs): po bzhugs pa dang / rang 'byung 'dren pa mya ngan gang 'das dang / rang rgyal gang dang nyan thos gang yod pa/ thams cad rang 'byung gi ni sman gyis gzigs/
104a8(dkon brtsegs): byang chub sems dpa' srog chags phan 'dod pa/ gang dag byang chub spod la mchog spod cing / la la zhig med gnas ni rtogs 'gyur ro/ thams cad rang byung
104b1(dkon brtsegs): 'drin pa dag gis gzigs/ gang gi srog chags shing du pra mthong ba/ bde gshegs mig ni 'di 'dra dri ma med/ mig stobs bsam gyi mi khyab dgu pa ste/ rgyal
104b2(dkon brtsegs): sras nges pa rnams ni mngon par dang / sha ri'i bu 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs dgu pa ste/ stobs de dang ldan pas khyu mchog
104b3(dkon brtsegs): gi gnas su zhal gyis phyi zhing / 'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par sgrog pa nas/ sus kyang 'jig rten 'dir chos dang mthun pa zhes bya ba'i bar du'o// de la de
104b4(dkon brtsegs): bzhin gshegs pa'i zag pa zad pa mngon sum du byed pa mkhyen pa'i stobs/ gang zhe na/ 'di la sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa bla na med pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye she
104b5(dkon brtsegs): kyi stobs kyi zag pa thams cad pas bdag skye bo ni zad/ tshangs par spong pa la ni bstan/ bya ba ni byas 'di las srid pa gzhan mi shes so// zhes zag pa med pa/ sems
104b6(dkon brtsegs): can par grol ba/ rang gi mngon par shes pas mngon sum du byas nas rdzogs par byas te gnas pa de la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i zag pa zad pa'i mkhyen pa'i stobs
104b7(dkon brtsegs): de ni/ bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba thams cad yang dag par bcom mo// nyan thos kyi thegs pa'i zag pa zad pa ni/ tshad du byas pa'i bag chags yang dag par
104b8(dkon brtsegs): bcom pa'o// rang sangs rgyas kyi zag pa zad pa ni tshad yod snying rje chen po dang bral ba spobs pa dang bral ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i zag pa zad pa ni/ rnams
105a1(dkon brtsegs): @pa thams cad kyang mchog dang ldan pa/ bag chags kyi 'tshams sbyor ba thams cad yang dag par bcom
105a2(dkon brtsegs): pa snying rje chen pos kun bzang ba mi 'jig pa dang / spobs pa la lta ba 'jig rten thams cad kyis zil gyi mi non pa ste/ skad cig gcig dang ldan pa'o// de ci'i phyir
105a3(dkon brtsegs): zhe na/ de bzhin gshegs pa la las kyi bag chags med/ nyon mongs pa'i bag chags med/ spyod lam 'khrul pa'i bag chags med do// 'di lta ste/ sha ri'i
105a4(dkon brtsegs): bun mkha' yongasu dag pas/ rdul dang du ba'i 'khrug pa dang lhan gcig tu mi gnas pa de bzhin du/ sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa'i zag pa zad pa mkhyen pa'i
105a5(dkon brtsegs): stobs kyang nyon mongs pa'i bag chags thams cad lhan cig tu mi gnas pa'o// de zag pa zad pa mkhyen pa de lta bu la rab tu gnas nas/ zag pa dang bcas pa/
105a6(dkon brtsegs): len pa dang bcas pa'i sems can rnams la zag pa zad par bya ba'i chos sto to// len pa spangs pa'i phyir chos ston te/ kyai sems can rnams ni yang dag pa ma
105a7(dkon brtsegs): yin pa kun tog pa las byung ste/ zag pa deng len pa rnams mi bskyed pa'i phyir yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du khyed kyi rab tu rtogs shis ces/ de dag la de bzhin gshegs
105a8(dkon brtsegs): pas dpe dang tshul gyis ci nas kyang zag pa rnams yang dag pa ma yin pa'o zhes yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin rab tu shes par 'gyur zhing shes nas kyang / chos gang
105b1(dkon brtsegs): yang mi len te/ len pa med par yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar 'gyur ba de lta de lta bur chos ston to// de ltar sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pas
105b2(dkon brtsegs): sems can thams cad zug pa rnams rab tu mkhyen to// zag pa kun tu 'byung ba dang / zag pa 'gag pa dang / zag pa 'gyur ba'i lam yang dag par ji lta ba
105b3(dkon brtsegs): bzhin rab tu mkhyen te/ mkhyen nas de bzhin du chos ston to// byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i zag pa zad pa mngon sum byed pa'i mkhyen pa'i stobs de
105b4(dkon brtsegs): thos nas mngon par dad/ yid ches rab tu rtogs/ som nyid med cing the tsom mi za nas/ ngo mtshar dang smad kyi bar du 'du shes bskyed do// 'di la chos
105b5(dkon brtsegs): nyid ni 'di yin te/ de la 'di skad ces bya'o// 'dren pa'i zag pa med pa'i ye shes ni/ rgya chen sgrib med pa dag pa tshad med de/ stobs bcu'i stobs ni de dang ldan
105b6(dkon brtsegs): pas na/ zhi ba'i byang chub mchog 'di rab tu gsungs/ nyan thos rnams kyis zag zad ye shes ni/ bag chags ma bcom tshang dang ldan pa yin/
105b7(dkon brtsegs): mi'i dam pa 'dren pa mchog rab kyi/ bag chags bcom zhing tshad dang ldan pa yin/ de bzhin rang rgyal byang chub gang reg pa/ de la snying rje che dang spobs pa med/ bco
105b8(dkon brtsegs): ldan 'das ni zag pa yongs zad pa/ snying rje che dang spobs pa tshad med do// sangs rgyas zag zad mkhyen la gnas nas ni/ 'gro ba'i zag pa yang dag ma yin zhing /
106a1(dkon brtsegs): rigs pa'i gnas kyi tshul 'di shes pas/ chos 'di thams cad logs par zhugs mkhyen te/
106a2(dkon brtsegs): de la rgyal ba'i snying rje cher skyed nas/ chos 'di ma rtag stong pa bdag med chos/ dngos med bsog ste mchog tu zhi ba'i/ sa la gtogs shing stos shes rab tu ston/
106a3(dkon brtsegs): 'di la skyes bu srog dang gang zag dang / shed skyes shed bu byed pa po yang med/ chos 'di thams cad log par chags pa na/ ston pas snying rjes bskyed nas thar ston kyang /
106a4(dkon brtsegs): bde bar gshegs la skyo ba yongs med de/ yang dag ye shes rnams kyang nyams pa med/ de phyir rgyal ba rtag tu rnal 'byor spor/ 'gro la phan phyir chos rnams rab tu ston//
106a5(dkon brtsegs): 'di ni pha rol smra ba 'joms pa'i stobs/ mtha' yas na mkha' 'dra ba bcu pa ste/ mgon po stobs bcu de la gnas gyur nas/ mtshungs med 'khor lo dam pa rab tu bskor/
106a6(dkon brtsegs): sha ri'i bu de bzhir gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu pa ste/ stobs de dang ldan pas de bzhin gshegs pas khyu mchog gi gnas su zhal gyi 'ches zhing
106a7(dkon brtsegs): 'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par sgrog ste/ 'jig rten 'dir dge sbyong ngam/ bram ze'i bar du sus kyang chos dang mthun par rab tu ma bskor ba/ tshangs pa'i 'kho
106a8(dkon brtsegs): lo rab tu bskor ro// de ltar sha ri'i bu byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams la mngon/
106b1(dkon brtsegs): par dad / yid ches/ rab tu rtog pa ngo mtshar dang rbad kyi rab tu 'du shes pa bskyed do// bam po drug pa'o// /
106b2(dkon brtsegs): yang sha ri'i bu ji ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jig pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa la mngon par dang / yid ces rab tu
106b3(dkon brtsegs): rtog/ som nyid med/ the tsom mi za nas/ ngo mtshar dang rmad kyi bar du 'du shes bskyed ces na/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa'i ni bzhi po
106b4(dkon brtsegs): 'di dag ste/ mi 'jig pa de dag dang ldan pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par sgrog cing / khru mchog gi gnas su zhal gyi 'che ste/ dge sbyong ngam/
106b5(dkon brtsegs): bram ze 'am/ bdud dam sus kyang 'jig rten du chos dang mthun par ma skor ba'i tshangs pa'i 'khor lo rab tu bskor ro// gzhi gang zhe na/ 'di la sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa

113a7(dkon brtsegs): bar byed pa/ 'khor thams cad kyis lus sim par byed pa/ 'khor thams cad kyi sems tshim par bskyed pa/ 'khor thams cad dga' ba dang / rab tu dga' ba dang /
113a8(dkon brtsegs): dad pa skyed pa snying rje chen pos sbyor ba de bzhin nyid kyi mnyam pa de kho na nyid/ de bzhin nyid/ gzhan ma yin pa nyid/ mi 'gyur ba nyid/ mi 'khrugs pa nyid/ 'byung ba med pa nyid//
113b1(dkon brtsegs): 'jig pa med pa nyid/ brtsod pa med pa nyid de/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'jigs pa la rtsod pa gang yang med do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa ni/
113b2(dkon brtsegs): rtsod pa med pa/ zab pa med pa'o// de bzhin nyid dang / mnyam zhing chos kyi dbyings kyi ngos mnyam pa/ 'jigs rten gyi khams rab 'byems ma lus pa thams cad la thog
113b3(dkon brtsegs): pa med pa'o// de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa tshad med grangs med bsam gyis mi khyab gzhal du med dpag tu med/ brjod du med pa'i chos dang ldan zhing snying rje chen pos zin gyi
113b4(dkon brtsegs): sems kyi sems can rnams la nges par 'byung ba'i lam yang dag par rab tu ston te/ des so sor rtogs pas/ sems can der 'jug pa rnams de byed pa'i sdug
113b5(dkon brtsegs): bsngal yang dag par zad cing nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// sha ri'i bu 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa bzhi po ste//
113b6(dkon brtsegs): mi 'jigs pa de dang ldan pas de bzhin gshegs pa 'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par sgrogs cing / khyu mchog gi gnas su zhal gyi 'che ste/ dge slo ngam/
113b7(dkon brtsegs): bram ze 'am/ lha 'am/ bdud dam/ tshang pa 'am/ sus kyang 'jig rten 'dir chos dang mthun par ma sbyor ba tshangs pa'i 'khor lo rab tu skor ro// de ltar sha ri'i bu de
113b8(dkon brtsegs): bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa bzhi yang mtha' yas mu med do// 'di lta ste dper na/ sha ri'i bu na mkha' mtha' yas mu med pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi
114a1(dkon brtsegs): / 'jigs pa bzhi yang mtha' ya sa mu med de sems can thams cad kyi zad par mi 'gyur ro// sha ri'i bu ga de
114a2(dkon brtsegs): bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa'i mtha' 'dod pa'i de ni na mkha'i mtha' 'dod do// byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i
114a3(dkon brtsegs): mi 'jigs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa de zos nas mngon par dad yid ches rab tu rdzogs/ som nyid med/ the tshom mi za/ rgya cher dga' mgu ste/ rangs pa rnyed
114a4(dkon brtsegs): nas na mkha' lta bur bsam gyi mi khyab pa'i phyir ngo mtshar dang slad du 'du shes bskyed do// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag gsung so//
114a5(dkon brtsegs): chos kun mnyam pa nyid mnyam par/ rang 'byung bas ni rjes su rtogs/ de phyir yang dag rdzogs sangs rgyas/ de bzhin gshegs pa mnyam pa gzigs/
114a6(dkon brtsegs): so so'i skye bo chos gang yin/ de dag sangs rgyas chos dang mnyam/ slob dang mi slob chos rnams dang / rang rgyal gyis ni chos nyid dang / gang dag 'jig rten
114a7(dkon brtsegs): 'das chos dang / dge dang mi dag mi g.yo rnams/ mya ngan 'das pa'i lam dang 'dra/ stong pa nyid dang mtshan med/ smon lam dag ni rnam par spangs/
114a8(dkon brtsegs): ma skyes mngon par 'du mi byed/ 'di ni mnyam pa nyid du bsten/ 'di dag mnyam pa nyid rtogs nas/ thub pa chen po mi 'jigs pa/ gang gi sems can 'gro la
114b1(dkon brtsegs): 'gyur ba/ de bzhin du yang rab tu ston/ 'jig rten gsum las rnam par grol/ rnam par thar pa rab tu ston/ mi dbang gis ni mi 'jigs pa/ gnyis pa yang dag
114b2(dkon brtsegs): rab tu stan/ rgyal bas gang chos rjes su sangs rgyas pa/ ma bsten par ni rnam par grol mi thob/ bag med dang khrel ba med 'gyur dang / gang la ngo tsha ni yang med pa dang /
114b3(dkon brtsegs): lus dang ngag rnams dang ni yid kyis su/ gang dag sdom pa rnams yang yod min dang / bdun dang zhe sdang gti mug 'jigs pa dang / srod gcod pa dang gzhan la
114b4(dkon brtsegs): kha dang / gzhan gyi chung pa de bzhin rdzun dang 'chang / nga rgyal mi gus de ni bdun pa'o// gang dag log par smra ba brgyad pa ste/ thams cad rnam par grol ba'i la
114b5(dkon brtsegs): rgyun gcod/ gang dag mnar med dog dang nyes mang dang / me dge bcu'i las kyi lam rnams dang / gang dag tshul min zhi ba mi shes pa/ de dag la ni rnam yang zar
114b6(dkon brtsegs): kha med/ phyin ci log la zhugs par rigs 'gyur nas/ bag med yang dag ma yin spu la chags/ rgyal ba rnams kyi mi 'jigs gsum pa ste/ chos nyid 'di
114b7(dkon brtsegs): dag la ni bsnyen par bya/ gang dag rnam dpyod sgon chad med la/ mi gang sten pa byang chub reg par 'gyur/ rgyal ba nyid kyi ma thos thams cad rig shes nas pa
114b8(dkon brtsegs): mchir 'gro ba'i chos 'chad do// cin pa dge ba'i chos yod pa/ byang chub phyogs dge rgyal bas bsngags pa la/ rjed pa rnam par thar pa mi 'thong pa/ gnas re
115a1(dkon brtsegs): pa ni skabs bcu rnams kyi bshad/ tshul bzhin du ni nyon mongs mang po na/ yang dag chos dge mnyam pa med ldan zhing /
115a2(dkon brtsegs): chos dang chos ma yin la de mi chags/ zhi ba mya ngan med pa rnam grol reg/ gsog gsob na mkha' 'dra zhing ya ma rA/ sgyu ma'i gzugs 'dra nam mkha'i lta bu dang /
115a3(dkon brtsegs): dge chos rnam pa gang gis rab shes pa/ de ni srid pa'i mtsho las thar bar 'gyur/ nub pa stobs bcu rnams kyi chos 'di ni/ 'gro ba'i gang mos srid par grol ba la/
115a4(dkon brtsegs): snying rje snying rtse byas nas thar byed de/ mi 'jig bzhi pa na mkha' 'dra ba'o// de ltar sha ri'i bu byang chub sems dpa' mi 'jigs pa bsam gyis mi khyab la mngon par
115a5(dkon brtsegs): dad yid ches rab tu rtog/ som nyid med/ the tshom mi za ba nas/ na mkha' lta bur bas gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir ngo mtshar smad kyi bar tu 'du shes bskyed do// /
115a6(dkon brtsegs): shwa ri bu ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po bsam gyis mi khyab pa la mngon dang/
115a7(dkon brtsegs): yid ches rab tu rtog som nyid med/ the tshos pi za ba nas/ ngo mtshar zad kyi bar du 'du shes bskyed ce na/ 'di la sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pa rnams
115a8(dkon brtsegs): kyi snying rje chen po ni sems can thams cad rjes su mi gtong zhing / rtag tu 'jug pa/ sems can yongs su smin par 'gyur ba ste/ mi ldog par rig par bya'o// /
115b1(dkon brtsegs): de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po de yang / ji ltar ngag gi las kyang khong du chud par bya ba sla ba ma yin pa de ltar tshad med/ de ltar mtshungs pa med/ de ltar dpag
115b2(dkon brtsegs): tu med/ de ltar brjod du med/ de ltar mi zad cing khong du chud par dka'o smo// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pas/ byang chub thob pa de ltar/ sems
115b3(dkon brtsegs): can la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po 'jug ste/ byang chub ji 'dra ba snying rje chen po yang de 'dra'o// de bzhin gshegs pas byang chub ci ltar thob ce na/ de bzhin
115b4(dkon brtsegs): gshegs pas rtsa ba med pa gnas med pa'i byang chub thob po// de la rtsa ba gang gnas gang zhe na/ 'jig tshogs ni rtsa ba'o// yang dag pa ma yin pa/ kun tu rtog pa ni
115b5(dkon brtsegs): gnas so// de bzhin gshegs pa'i byang chub mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir de dag mnyam par mkhyen te/ de'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pas rtsa ba med pa gnas med pa'i byang chub
115b6(dkon brtsegs): mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas zhes bya ste/ sems can 'di dag rtsa ba med pa gnas med pa'i mi shes pas/ de dag shes par bya'o// zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin
115b7(dkon brtsegs): gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po 'jug go// gzhan yang sha ri'i bu byang chub ni zhi ba nye bar zhi ba'o// de ji ltar zhi ba nye bar zhi zhes na/ nang zhi ba'o// phyi rol nye bar
115b8(dkon brtsegs): zhi ba'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ mig ni bdag dang bdag gis stong ste/ de'i rang bzhin 'di yin pas de'i phyir zhi ba zhes bya'o// de bzhin du rna ba dang / sa sA dang lce dang /
116a1(dkon brtsegs): lus dang / yid ni bdag dang bdag gis stong/ de'i rang bzhin 'di yin pas na de'i phyir zhi ba zhes
116a2(dkon brtsegs): bya'o// de mig stong yongs su shes nas/ gzugs la mi rgyug ste/ de'i phyir nye bar zhi ba zhes bya'o// yid kyi bar du yang stong par yongs su shes nas/ chos
116a3(dkon brtsegs): la mi rgyug ste/ de'i phyir nye bar zhi ba zhes bya'o// sems can 'di dag ni zhi ba dang nye bar zhi ba mi shwe te/ de dag shes bya'o zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs
116a4(dkon brtsegs): pa'i snying rje chen po la 'dzag go/ gzhan yang sha ri'i bu des ni rang bzhin gyi 'od gsal bar byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// ji ltar 'od gsal zhe
116a5(dkon brtsegs): na rang bzhin gang yin pa de ni kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa ste/ nam mkha' lta bu'o// na mkha'i rang bzhin ni na mkha'i rjes su 'brang ba'o// na mkha' dang mnyam pa nyid
116a6(dkon brtsegs): kyis mnyam pa ste/ de ni rang bzhin gyis shin du 'od gsal ba/ rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba 'di khong du ma chud pas byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams/ blo bur
116a7(dkon brtsegs): gyis nyon mongs pas kun nas nyon mongs pa ste/ sems can rnams rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba 'di mi shes pa de dag rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba khong du chud par
116a8(dkon brtsegs): bya'o// zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po 'jug go// gzhan yang sha ri'i bu ngas ni blang ba med pa dang / dor ba med par byang chub mngon
116b1(dkon brtsegs): par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// de la blang ba med pa gang dor ba med pa gang zhes na/ blang ba med pa zhes bya ba ni/ chos thams cad mi 'dzin pa'o// dor ba med pa zhes
116b2(dkon brtsegs): bya ba ni/ chos thams cad rab tu 'dzin pa med pa'o// de la de bzhin gshegs pas blang ba med pa dang / dor ba med pa chu bo mnyam pa nyid du gzigs te/ ji ltar
116b3(dkon brtsegs): de bzhin gshegs pas tshul rol med pa dang / pha rol med par gzigs pa de ltar chos thams cad tshu rol dang pha rol dang bral bar de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par rdzogs
116b4(dkon brtsegs): par sangs rgyas te/ de'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa zhes bya'o// blang ba med pa dang / dor ba med pa'i sems can sems can rnams kyi khong du chud pas bya'o zhes
116b5(dkon brtsegs): sems can rnams la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po 'jug go// gzhan yang sha ri'i bu des mtshan ma med pa dang / dmigs pa med pa'i byang chub
116b6(dkon brtsegs): mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// de la mtshan ma med pa gang / dmigs pa med pa gang zhe na/ mig gi rnam par shes pa mi dmigs pa ni mtshan ma med pa'o// /
116b7(dkon brtsegs): gzugs la yang rjes su mi mthong ba ni dmigs so// yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i bar du mi dmigs pa ni mtshan ma med pa'o// chos yang dag par rjes su mi
116b8(dkon brtsegs): mthong ba ni dmigs pa med pa'o// de ltar sha ri'i bu mtshan ma med pa dang / dmigs pa med pa'i 'phags pa rnams kyi spyod yul lo// 'phags pa rnams
117a1(dkon brtsegs): kyi spyod yul gang zhe na/ khams gsum pa ni 'phags pa rnams kyi spyod yul te/ gang 'phags pa rnams kyi
117a2(dkon brtsegs): spyod yul de ni/ byis pa so so'i thams cad kyi spyod yul ma yin pas/ de khong du chud par bya'o// zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po
117a3(dkon brtsegs): la 'jug go/ sha ri'i bu byang chub ni 'das pa ma yin/ ma 'ongs pa ma yin pa/ da ltar byung ba ma yin te/ dus gsum mnyam pa 'khor gsum yongs su chad
117a4(dkon brtsegs): pa'o// de la 'khor gsum yongs su chad pa gang zhe na/ gang 'das pa la sems mi 'jug pa dang / ma 'ongs pa la rnam par shes pa rjes su mi rgyud pa dang / da ltar
117a5(dkon brtsegs): byung ba la yid la byed pa mi 'jug pa ste/ de sems dang yid dang rnam par shes pa la mi gnas pas/ 'das pa la ma rtogs/ ma 'ongs pa la rlom sems
117a6(dkon brtsegs): su mi byed/ da ltar byung ba la spros par mi byed pa 'di ni du gsum mnyam pa nyid 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa yin na/ sems can rnams kyi khong du ma chud
117a7(dkon brtsegs): bas/ de khong du chud par bya'o// zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po 'jug go// sha ri'i bu ngas byang chub ni lus med pa mngon par
117a8(dkon brtsegs): 'dus ma byas par mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ de ni mig gi rnam par shes pas/ rnam par shes par bya ba ma yin pa nas/ yid kyi rnam par shes
117b1(dkon brtsegs): pa'i bar gyis rnam par shes par bya ba ma yin no// 'dus ma byas shes bya ba ni gang pa skyes pa/ mi 'jigs pa mi gnas pa de ni 'khor gsum dang bral ba 'dus/
117b2(dkon brtsegs): ma byas shes bya'o// 'dus ma byas ji lta bar 'dus byas kyang de ltar khong du chud par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gang chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin de ni dngos po med
117b3(dkon brtsegs): pa'o// gang dngos po med pa de ni dngos po med pa'o// gang dngos po med pa de la ga med de/ lus med pa/ mngon par 'dus ma byas pa de sems can rnams kyis
117b4(dkon brtsegs): khong du chud pas/ de khong du chud par bya'o// zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po 'jug go/ sha ri'i bu ngas byang chub ni dbyer med pa'i gnas
117b5(dkon brtsegs): su mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// de la dbyer med pa gang gnas gang zhe na/ de bzhin nyid ni gnas so// gnas med pa ni dbyer bla'o// chos kyi dbyings ni
117b6(dkon brtsegs): gnas so// tha dad pa med ni dbyer med pa'o// yang dag pa'i mtha' ni gnas so// g.yo ba med pa ni dbyer med pa'o// stong pa nyid ni gnas so// dmigs su
117b7(dkon brtsegs): med pa ni dbyer med pa'o// mtshan ma med pa ni gnas so// rnam par mi rtog pa ni dbyer med pa'o// smon pa med pa ni gnas so// 'jug pa med pa ni dbyer med pa'o//
117b8(dkon brtsegs): sems can med pa ni gnas so// sems sred pa'i rang bzhin ni dbyer med pa'o// namakha' ni gnas so// mi dmigs pa ni dbyer med pa'o// mi skye ba ni gnas so//
118a1(dkon brtsegs): ji 'gug pa ni dbye med pa'o// 'dus ma byas ni gnas so// rgyu ba med pa ni dbyer med pa'o// byang chub ni gnas/
118a2(dkon brtsegs): nye bar zhi ba ni dbyer med pa'o// mya ngan las 'das pa ni gnas so// mngon par mi 'grub pa ni dbyer med pa'o// de ltar sha ri'i bu dbyer med pa'i gnas 'di sems can na
118a3(dkon brtsegs): kyis khong du ma chud pas/ de khong du chud par bya'o zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen pos 'jug go/ sha ri'i bu byang chub ni lus kyis mngon
118a4(dkon brtsegs): yar rdzogs par sangs ma rgyas te/ sems kyis kyang ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ lus ni bam po g.yo ba med pa byed pa/ rtsa dang rtsig pa dang shing dang rdo dang / mig yor
118a5(dkon brtsegs): lta bu'o// sems ni sgyu ma dang / smig sgyu dang / chu zla lta bu ste/ gang gis lus dang sems de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang chub ces bya'o// byang chub ni lus sam sems sam chos
118a6(dkon brtsegs): sem/ chos ma yin pa'am/ yang dag pa'am/ yang dag pa ma yin pa 'ab/ bden pa 'am/ rdzun pa gang gis kyang brjod par bya ba ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub
118a7(dkon brtsegs): ni chos thams cad kyis brjod par bya ba ma yin te/ byang chub la gang gis kyang tshig gi za snyed du 'gyur ba'i gnas cung zad kyang med do// ji ltar na mkha' gnas med cing
118a8(dkon brtsegs): tshig med de/ de bzhin du/ byang chub kyang gnas med pa brjod par bya ba ma yin pa'o// de ltar sha ri'i bu yang dag pa ji ltar ba bzhin du tshol ba mthams cad tshig med pa ste/
118b1(dkon brtsegs): chos tshig med/ tshig la chos med do// de lta bu'i chos kyi tshul mi shes shing khong du ma chud pa/ de khong du chud par bya'o zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying
118b2(dkon brtsegs): rje chen po 'jug go/ sha ri'i bu byang chub ni bzung ba med kun tu gzhi med pa'o// de la bzung ba med pa gang / kun gzhi med gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ mig yongs su shes
118b3(dkon brtsegs): pa ni gzung ba med pa'o// gzugs yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ba ni kun gzhi med pa'o// yid kyis bar du yongs su shes pa ni gzung ba med pa'o// chos ni dmigs pa
118b4(dkon brtsegs): ni kun gzhi med pa ste/ de ltar shA ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pas bzung ba med pa/ kun gzhi med par byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// mngon par rdzog par sa
118b5(dkon brtsegs): rgyas nas mig mi 'dzin pa dang / gzugs kun gizha med pas rnam par shes pa gnas so// yid kyi bar du mi 'dzin cing / chos kun gzhi med par shes pa mi gnas so//
118b6(dkon brtsegs): de rnam par shes myi gnas pas sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi gnas shes so// ji ltar shes ce na/ sems can rnams kyi sems kyi gnas ni 'di bzhi ste/ bzhig
118b7(dkon brtsegs): zhen/ 'di lta ste/ gzugs ni sems kyi gnas so// tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed ni sems can rnams kyi ni sems gnas te/ 'di bzhi ni sems can dam/
118b8(dkon brtsegs): kyi sems kyi gnas so// gnas de yang gnas med par de bzhin gshegs pas mkhyen to// gnas med pa'i mtha' 'di sems can rnams kyis khod du chud pas/ de khong dud
119a1(dkon brtsegs): par bya'o zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po 'jug go// sha ri'i bu byang chub ces bya ba ni stong pa
119a2(dkon brtsegs): nyid kyi tshig bla dgas so// stong pa nyid gang gis byang chub stong pa stong pa nyid des chos thams cad stong ste/ de dag stong pa ji lta ba bzhin du/ de ltar de bzhin gshegs
119a3(dkon brtsegs): pa'i chos thams cad mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas mod kyi/ stong pa nyid kyis stong pa nyid mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa ni ma yin pas/ stong pa nyid dam byang
119a4(dkon brtsegs): chub ces bya ba 'di ni tshul gcig pa'i ye shes so// de la gnyis po gang gis stong pa nyid dang byang chub tu gnyis su dbye ba'i gang yang med do// chos de ni gnyis su med cing
119a5(dkon brtsegs): dbyer med de/ ming med pa mtshan ma med pa/ 'jug pa med pa/ rab tu rgyu ba med pa/ sprod pa med pa'o// gang stong pa zhes bya ba ni/ mngon par chags pa dang / 'dzin
119a6(dkon brtsegs): pa dang / bral ba'o// don dam par chos gang yang mi dmigs te/ stong pa gang yin pa de stong pa zhes bya'o// ji ltar na mkha' na mkha' zhes kyang bya la na mkha' ni brjed
119a7(dkon brtsegs): par bya ba yang ma yin no// de bzhin du stong pa zhes kyang bya la/ stong pa nyid brjod par bya ba ma yin no// 'di lta ste/ ming tsam du tha snyed 'dogs pa 'di ni chos
119a8(dkon brtsegs): thams cad 'jug pa ste/ ming de yang yul na mi gnas phyogs na mi gnas so// ji ltar ming yul na mi gnas phyogs na mi gnas pa de bzhin du chos kyi ming gis tha snyed
119b1(dkon brtsegs): du 'dogs pa'i chos de yang yul na mi gnas phyogs na mi gnas te/ de ltar de bzhin gshegs pas chos thams cad mkhyen te/ thog ma nas ma skyes ma byung bar de ltar
119b2(dkon brtsegs): mkhyen pas de ltar rnam par grol te bcings pa ya med/ grol ba yang med/ de byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams kyis khong du ma chud pas/ de khong du chud par bya'o// /
119b3(dkon brtsegs): zhes sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po 'jug go/ sha ri'i bu byang chub ni na mkha' dang mnyam ste/ namakhe'i ni mnyam pa'ang ma yin//
119b4(dkon brtsegs): mi mnyam pa 'ang ma yin no// byang chub kyang mnyam pa yang ma yin mi mnyam pa'ang ma yin te/ ji ltar chos rnams yang dag par yongs su grub pa med pa de mnyam pa'ang //
119b5(dkon brtsegs): mi mnyam pa zhes brjod pa ma yin no// sha ri'i bu de bzhin gshegs pas chos thams cad mnyam pa'ang ma yin/ mi mnyam pa yang ma yin par mngon par rdzogs par
119b6(dkon brtsegs): sangs rgyas so// ji ltar chos rdul rtsa ma yang mnyam par byas pa'ang ma yin/ mi mnyam par byas pa yang ma yin pa de ltar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// /
119b7(dkon brtsegs): chos ji snyed pa de yang dag pa'i ye shes kyi shes so// yang dag pa'i ye shes gang zhe na/ chos ma byung ba rnams 'byung ba dang / byung nas 'jig par 'gyur

126b3(dkon brtsegs): gang mnyam par ba zhig kyang rung / mnyam par ma bzhag kyang rung ste/ su yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sems lta bar nus pa med do// ji ltar de bzhin
126b4(dkon brtsegs): gshegs pa'i rtags tu mnyam par bzhag pa de ltar ting nge 'dzin dag lta bas sems can rnams la chos ston te/ 'di ni gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos ma

126b6(dkon brtsegs): pa la med de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ nam mkha' bzhin du mi zad pa'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhing tha dad pa'i 'du shes med do// rang bzhin gyis tha dad pa med
126b7(dkon brtsegs): ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa la sems can tha dad pa'i 'dus shes med do/ chos kyi dbyer med mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi phyir/ de gshegs pa la sangs
126b8(dkon brtsegs): kyi rgyas kyi zhing tha dad pa'i 'du shes med do// 'dod chags dang bral ba yi chos nyid kyi phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa la chos tha dad pa'i 'du shes med de//
127a1(dkon brtsegs): de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa'i sems can la yang rjes su chags pa med/

127a7(dkon brtsegs): gshegs pa'i btang snyoms ni sems sdom pa dang / tshul khrims sgom pa dang / shes rab bsgoms pa'i yin te/ shes rab ma sgoms pa'i ma yin no//

160a3(dkon brtsegs): pa dang ni ldan par bya/ byang chub phyir ni slob dpon la rim gro dang ni sti stang bya/ 'das pa'i dus kyi bkral pa bsam med nas/ 'khor ba'i 'khor los yongs su
160a4(dkon brtsegs): khyam na/ skye mched ngag ni don med 'das gyur te/ sbyin gnas dag ni nye bar mtsho ba min/ dge ba'i gshes rnyen yongs su spangs 'gyur nas/ rtag tu rdeg pa'i
160a5(dkon brtsegs): grogs po rab stan te/ de dag gi ni snun pa'i rjes su 'jug cing / rgyun mi tshad par ngan song sa la gnas/ rtsa ba ni cing sdig pa rnams/ byed du bcug cing
160a6(dkon brtsegs): gzhan la spyod byas nas/ de'i 'bras bu ngan sang skye gnas 'gro/ rdig pa'i las ni sdug bsngal rjes su myong / dge ba'i gshes spen rnam ni matan pas/
160a7(dkon brtsegs): rnga rmo ba yang de bzhin bong bu yis/ dran pa'i tshams kyi skye mched bzung gyur nas/ dbyig pa bdag gi rdeg shing khal yA skal/ mir gyur pa ni shin du rnyed ka dang /
160a8(dkon brtsegs): dzu bI'i yul dang dge ba'i gshes spen rnyeng / shin tu yuni ring dam par gyur te/ ka ba'i las kyi bu gar chud pa bzhin/ lus dang ngag ni shin du snga ma gyur nas/
160b1(dkon brtsegs): zhan pa med pa'i sems kyi rtson 'grus brtsa ba/ dge ba'i gshes snyen dag la g.yo med pas/ bdag gi lus ni nye bar mtsho bar bya/ bdag gis slob dpon
160b2(dkon brtsegs): bla ma kang dgu dang / gang dag bdag gis byang chub sems bskyed pa/ byang chub dam pa mchog gi lam ston pa/ ston pa bzhin du dga' bas brnyen bkur bya/
160b3(dkon brtsegs): rnam pa sna chags dag gi byug pa dang / dri dang phye ma rnam pa sna tshogs dang / gos dang me tog dag gi rgyun pa yis/ rkang gnyis dam pa la ni mchod par bya/ phyogs
160b4(dkon brtsegs): bcu dag na sangs rgyas gang bzhugs pa/ sems can don la brtson zhing don dam gzigs/ gsar gyi kha dog lta bur 'od dzes pa/ kha dog mtha' yas pa la mchod
160b5(dkon brtsegs): par bya/ sangs rgyas mi'i kha lo sgyur rnams la/ 'jig rten spyod dang mchod pa chen byas pa la/ gang gis byang chub snying por bdug 'gro ba'i/ byang chub
160b6(dkon brtsegs): lam ni shin du sbyangs par 'gyur/ shA ri'i bu sems sred pa bzhi pa 'di bskyed nas/ byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod kyi chos kyi rnam grangs
160b7(dkon brtsegs): yongs su tshol bas/ slob dpon la rim gro dang / bsnyen bkur byed do/ zan chu bum pa gang tsam yang 'bul lo// gzhan yang sha ri'i bu byang chub
160b8(dkon brtsegs): sems dpa' 'di ltar sems bskyed do// bdag yun ring por dge ba'i shas spen dang bral zhing sdig pa'i grogs pos zin pas le lo can brtson 'grus

161a3(dkon brtsegs): bzhi las sdig pa med/ de'i bzhi las sdig pa'i rnam pa med do// rgya mtsho'i pha tshur rol gyi sems can ji snyed pa de dag thams cad sbyin pas tshim par byas kyang //
161a4(dkon brtsegs): de'i bzhi las bsod nams med// de'i bzhi las bsod nas kyi rnam pa med do// rgya mtsho'i pha rol gyi sems cad ji snyed pa de dag thams cad bsad cing gtubs
161a5(dkon brtsegs): kyang / de'i gzhi las sdig pa med pa/ de'i gzhi las sdig pa'i rnam pa med do snyems pas/ de ltar byas kyang bsod nams dang / sdig pas yongs su

161a8(dkon brtsegs): pas/ de na bdag ni sems can dmyal bar gyur pas/ lcags kyi thu lum sregs pa za zhing cig tu sdug bsngal ba rtsub pa'i mi bzad pa 'tshogs pa/ 'chi

162b4(dkon brtsegs): bya ba dang / ldang ba dang / thal mo smra ba'i las kyi rnam par smin pa med do// zhes de ltar mos pa'i bar gyis/ nga rgyal gyi zil gyis non pas sdig pa mi
162b5(dkon brtsegs): dge ba'i las mngon par 'dus byas te/ mi dge ba'i las de'i rnam par smin pas/ 'di lta ste/ mi'i nang du sbyin gnas thams cad nye bar 'tsho ba ma yin pa
162b6(dkon brtsegs): smad pa'i lus thob ste/ 'di lta bu'i sprin gnas mnyes par ma byas pas/ der bdag mir gyur pa na/ mi bkren pa dang dbul po dang / bran du gyur pa dang /

287b3(dkon brtsegs): kyi gnod du nye bar gnas pa yin no// sha ri'i bu de ltar na 'di ni tham pas 'di shes rab te/ de'i byin byang chub sems dpa'i rnams kyi thabs dang shes rab kyi mngon
287b4(dkon brtsegs): bar sgrub pa'i bsam gtan gyi pha rol du phyin pa zhes bya'o// sha ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni mngon par shes pa las nyams
287b5(dkon brtsegs): ba med par 'du shes su gyur pa'i las rnams kyang byed do// mngon par shes pas kyang rnam par rol la/ bya ba thams cad yongs su ston to// mngon par shes
287b6(dkon brtsegs): ba la yang rab tu gnas la 'jug pa chen po la yang 'jug par byed do// de'i mngon par shes pa de ni ye shes byed pa'o// 'jig rten las 'das pa'o//
287b7(dkon brtsegs): nges par byed pa'i cha dang 'thun pa'o// bya ba thams cad la rnam pa'i cho ga thams cad dang ldan pa'o// de'i mngon par shes pa de ni shes rab byed pa'o//

288a3(dkon brtsegs): rnams su gzugs thams cad kun ston pa'i// de'i mngon par shes pa de ni sngon gyi mthi'i sgra dang / mnyam pa nyid kyis sgra thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'o/
288a4(dkon brtsegs): de'i mngon par shes pa de ni rang bzhin mngon sum du mthong bas/ sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spor ba la rnam par lta'o// de'i mngon par shes pa de ni

321a4(dkon brtsegs): rtogs pa dang / phyir zhing yongs su tshol ba dang / sems la rnyog pa med pa dang / sgrib pa gnod pa dang / ltung ba las 'byung bar shes pa dang / 'grod pa
321a5(dkon brtsegs): med pa dang / kun nas ldang ba med pa dang / nan tan snying por byed pa dang / chos la gzhol ba dang / chos la bab pa dang / chos rtul ba dang / rtug par mgo
321a6(dkon brtsegs): la med 'bar ba lta bu dang / ye shes tshol ba de nyid la gnas pa dang / mi lhong ba dang / brtson 'grus mi gtong ba dang / khyad par du 'gro ba dang / 'du

321b2(dkon brtsegs): dang / rkyen la ye shes kyi rjes su rig pa dang / khrel yod pa dang / ngo tsha shes pa'i rgyan dang / sangs rgyas kyi 'gros rje su 'gro ba dang / mi shes pa sel ba dang / gti
321b3(dkon brtsegs): mug gi ling tog sel ba dang / shes rab kyi mig rnam par dag pa dang / blo rgya che ba dang / blo ma zhum pa dang / blo rab tu tha dad pa dang / mngon sum du shes pa dang /
321b4(dkon brtsegs): gzhan la rag ma lus pa'i yon tan dang / rang gi yon tan gyi mi snyebs pa dang / pha rol gyi yon tan la rtog pa dang / leg par bya ba'i las byed pa dang / las
321b5(dkon brtsegs): kyi rnams par smin pa la mi 'gal bar byed pa dang / las yongs su drag par shes pa ste/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i ye shes kyi tsho ga shes bya'o//
321b6(dkon brtsegs): gzhan yang ye shes kyi tshog ni sbyin pa bzhi ste/ chos smra ba la grol ba dang / smyug gu dang / snag tsa dang / glegs bam sbyin pa dang / chos smra ba la chos kyi stan sna tshogs
321b7(dkon brtsegs): sbyin pa dang / chos smra ba la rnyed pa dang / bkur sti dang / tshig su bcad pa thams cad sbyin pa dang / chos smra ba la chos kun bsdu ba'i phyir/ g.yo med par legs
321b8(dkon brtsegs): zhes bya ba sbyin te/ sbyin pa bzhi po de dag ni ye shes kyi chos stsogs par 'gyur ba'o// kun srung bzhi rnam ye shes kyi tshog stsogs par gyur te/ bzhi
322a1(dkon brtsegs): tshol ba la dran mi nya nas pa dang / rtogs pa la don rtogs pa'i rjes su gang zhe na/ chos sla ba rnams
322a2(dkon brtsegs): kyi lus yongs su srung ba dang / dge ba srung ba dang / yul dang ljongs su 'jug pa la yongs su srung ba dang / ngan pa'i dngos po'i yongs su srung ba te/

322a4(dkon brtsegs): ston pa dang / zang zing ti bar ston pa dang / byang chub nye bar ston pa dang / stobs lnga ye shes kyi chogs su 'gyur te/ lnga gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ mos pa'i phyir dad
322a5(dkon brtsegs): pa'i stobs dang / thos pa tshol ba'i phyir brtson 'grus kyi stobs dang / byang chub kyi sems mi rjed pa'i phyir dran pa'i stobs dang / mnyam pa nyid kyi chos la des

322a7(dkon brtsegs): shes kyi tshogs stsogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos la nges pa'i tshul khrims dang / chos la nges par rtog pa'i tshul khrims dang / byang chub tu sngo ba
322a8(dkon brtsegs): tshul khrims te/ tshul khrims bzhi po de dag ye shes kyi cho gas stsogs par 'gyur ro// bzhi ye shes kyi chos stsogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos che/
322b1(dkon brtsegs): ba la mngon par brtson pa ngan du smras pa dang / ngan du brjod pa'i tshig rnams bzod pa dang / chos tshol ba la mngon par rtson pas/ rlung dang tsha ba dang / grang ba dang dro ba dang /

322b4(dkon brtsegs): bzhi ye shes kyi tshogs stsogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ thos pa brtson 'grus dang / gzungs kyi brtson 'grus dang / snyan pa'i brtson 'grus dang /
322b5(dkon brtsegs): nan tan gyi brtson 'grus teng / 'di lta ste/ brtson 'gras bzhi po de dag ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs par 'gyur ro// bsam gtan gyi yan lag bzhi ye shes
322b6(dkon brtsegs): kyi tshogs rdzogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dben pa dang / cig pur dga' ba dang / ye shes dang mngon par shes pa tshol ba dang / sangs
322b7(dkon brtsegs): rgyas kyi ye shes la 'jug pa ste/ bsam gtan gyi yan lag bzhi po de dag ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs par 'gyur ro// shes rab snang ba'i chos 'di bzhi ye shes kyi
322b8(dkon brtsegs): tshogs rdzogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chad pal mi gnas pa dang / rtag pa la mi 'jug pa dang / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba dang /
323a1(dkon brtsegs): mi 'gal ba dang / bdag med pa la sems pa ste/ shes rab snang ba'i bzhi po de dag ye shes kyi

323a4(dkon brtsegs): shes kyi tshogs su 'gyur ro// chos 'di bzhi la mtshogs kyi ye shes la 'jug par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i lam dang /

323a6(dkon brtsegs): tshogs kyi ye shes la 'jug par 'gyur ro// mi ngom pa 'di bzhi ye shes kyi tshogs stsogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ thob par mi ngoms
323a7(dkon brtsegs): pa dang / snyan pas mi ngoms pa dang / dpyod pas mi ngoms pa dang / ye shes kyis mi ngoms pa ste/ mi ngoms pa bzhi po de dag ye shes kyi tshogs stsogs

323b6(dkon brtsegs): pa la spod do// de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dran pa nye bar bzhag pa la mkhas pa gang zhe na/ 'di bzhi ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dran pa nye bar

324a1(dkon brtsegs): bzhag pa slob pa'o// de la lus la lus kyi rjes su lta ba dran pa nye bar bzhag pasgom pa gang zhen/
324a2(dkon brtsegs): sha ri'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' lus la lus kyi rjes su lta zhing gnas pa te/ lus kyi sngon gyi mtha' la yang so sor rtog/ lus kyi phyir pa'i mtha'

355b1(dkon brtsegs): par bya/ gzhan dag la rgya cher yang dag par rab tu ston par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod kyi chos kyi rnam grangs shin du mnyan tam/ blangs sam/ bzung ngam
355b2(dkon brtsegs): ka na chub par byas sam/ gzhan dag la rgya cher yang dag par rab tu bstan na/ dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung rgyan ma bcad par bya ba'i phyir zhugs pa yin no// tshad med pa bzhi dang mi bral ba yin no/
355b3(dkon brtsegs): pha rol tu phyin pa drag la brtson pa yin no// bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi sems can rnams sdang ba la brtson pa la brtson pa yin no// sha ri'i bu gang 'di byang chu sems dpa'i sde snod kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'a
355b4(dkon brtsegs): byang chub kyi lam yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bla na med pa'i yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod kyi chos kyi rnam grangs dang 'brel to// sha ri'i bu byang chub sems dpas kyi rna
355b5(dkon brtsegs): byang chub sems dpa'i sde sdod kyi chos kyi rnam grangs kyi nang du bcu go/ sha ri'i bu byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod kyis 'di la bslab nas yang dag par chad pa rje su thob po// pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin
355b6(dkon brtsegs): pa gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi pha rol tu song ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad la nges par byas par de bzhin gshegs pa mdzod pa rgyun ma chad pa rnams
355b7(dkon brtsegs): thams cad kyis tshed bde pa'i rjesu thob pa/ de bzhin gshegs pas dpag tu med pa rjesu thob pa/ pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad rjes su thob pa/ pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad la shin du gnas pas/ de nas bcom ldan
355b8(dkon brtsegs): 'das kyis de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag gsungaso// las kyi las dang rnam smin gyis// rnam par smin pa shes par bya/ las min rnam smin ma yin gang // de bde de ni mya ngan 'das// gang la
356a1(dkon brtsegs): / shes pa med pa yin/ 'dus byas thams cad sdug bsngal te/ de phyir shes pa
356a2(dkon brtsegs): bskyed nas ni/ 'dis byas kun las rnam par grol/ bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/
356a3(dkon brtsegs): tshe dang ldan pa sha ri'i bu dang / dge slong de dag dang / lha dang mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri
356a4(dkon brtsegs): zabacas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung ba la mngon par bstod do//
356a5(dkon brtsegs): 'phags pa dkon mchog brtsegs pa chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs le'u stong phrag brgya pa las/
356a6(dkon brtsegs): byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod kyi le'u zhes pa ste le'u bcu gnyis pa rdzog ste sto/
356a7(dkon brtsegs): bkra shis/ dge'o//
